## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="e2189-825">Attributi di Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e2189-825">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e2189-826">Questa classe contiene gli attributi seguenti per Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e2189-826">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
